    제5편. 프레임 벤치마크 - 118개 물리식 전수 검증

    제11장. 검증 방법

    118개 물리식을 반야프레임에 대입하여 호환 여부를 검증하는 방법론을 정의한다.

    8.1 방법론

    gtest(단위 테스트)와 동일한 방식이다. 각 물리식을 반야프레임 프레임에 대입하여:

  • 1. 해당 식이 어느 괄호(서브프레임)에서 작동하는지 분류한다
  • 2. 반야프레임의 4축 직교 구조와 호환되는지 판정한다
  • 3. PASS/FAIL 결과를 기록한다

    • 호환 조건: 해당 식의 모든 물리량이 반야프레임의 4축(time, space, observer, superposition) 또는 그 조합으로 표현 가능해야 한다.

    8.2 서브프레임 분류

    서브프레임사용 축대응 물리
    space 서브프레임space만기하학, 역제곱 법칙
    time-space 서브프레임time + space역학, 상대성, 파동
    양자 서브프레임observer + superposition양자역학
    양쪽 걸침고전 + 양자양자장론, 인터페이스
    전체 프레임4축 전부우주론, 블랙홀 열역학

    제12장. 검증 결과 118개 요약

    118개 물리식(2차식 76개 + 비2차식 42개)을 반야프레임에 대입하여 전수 검증했다. 각 식마다 원래 수식, 반야프레임 변환식, 서브프레임 분류, 판정 사유를 기록했다. 상세 검증 내용은 본 보고서 말미의 부록에 수록되어 있다.

    검증 요약

    분야식 수PASSFAIL
    A. 고전역학880
    B. 중력880
    C. 전자기학12120
    D. 특수상대성770
    E. 양자역학10100
    F. 양자장론550
    G. 열역학770
    H. 파동역학550
    I. 유체역학330
    J. 광학440
    K. 일반상대성440
    L. 우주론330
    M. 1차식12120
    N. 3차 이상880
    O. 지수/로그880
    P. 텐서/행렬550
    Q. 1차 양자식330
    R. 원리/부등식660
    총합1181180

    FAIL 0개. 반야프레임 밖의 물리식은 발견되지 않았다.

    제13장. 벤치마크 집계

    118개 검증 결과를 분야별, 서브프레임별로 집계한다.

    10.1 환원 패턴 요약

    유형개수왜 호환되냐
    1차식12에너지로 보면 2차로 환원
    3차 이상82차의 도함수이거나 거듭제곱
    지수/로그8지수 안에 2차가 인자로 존재
    텐서5메트릭 자체가 2차 형식
    1차 양자식3제곱하면 2차, 관측량이 2차
    원리/부등식6프레임의 구조적 규칙

    비2차식은 전부 2차로 환원되거나, 2차량을 인자로 포함하거나, 프레임의 구조적 규칙이다.

    10.4 총합 판정

    2차식:    76/76 PASS (100%)
비2차식:  42/42 PASS (100%)
총합:    118/118 PASS (100%). FAIL 0개.

반야프레임 밖의 물리식은 발견되지 않았다.

    제6편. 총괄

    제14장. 기존 통합 시도와의 비교

    물리학은 고전과 양자를 합치기 위해 100년간 시도해왔다. 대표적인 두 접근과 반야프레임을 비교한다.

    끈이론은 1차원 끈의 진동 모드로 모든 입자와 힘을 설명하려 한다. 수학적으로 정합적이려면 10-11차원이 필요하며, 여분의 차원은 컴팩트화되어 관측 불가하다고 가정한다. 40년간 실험적 검증이 이루어지지 않았으며, 가능한 진공 상태가 10⁵^{0}^{0}개에 달해 예측력이 사실상 없다.

    루프양자중력은 시공간 자체를 이산적(양자화된) 구조로 본다. 공간이 플랑크 스케일에서 연속이 아니라 그물(네트워크)이라고 주장한다. 끈이론보다 차원 수는 적지만 아직 완성되지 않았으며, 표준 모델과의 통합이 미완이다.

    반야프레임은 합치려 하지 않는다. 고전과 양자가 직교한다고 선언한다. 합칠 수 없는 이유가 원래 직교(DATA와 OPERATOR)이기 때문이라는 답이다. 추가 차원이 필요 없고, 기존 118개 물리식과 100% 호환되며, 관측자 문제, 디코히어런스, 인과율, 암흑물질/에너지까지 하나의 프레임으로 설명한다.

    항목끈이론루프양자중력반야프레임
    접근합치려 함합치려 함직교로 선언
    차원10-11이산 시공간4축
    수학 복잡도극도로 복잡매우 복잡1줄
    실험 검증불가 (40년간)미완성118/118 호환
    관측자 문제미완미완해결 (CAS Read)
    디코히어런스별도 해석 필요별도 해석 필요CAS 커밋으로 해결
    인과율별도 가정내장내장 (해시체인)
    암흑물질/에너지별도 이론 필요별도 이론 필요LRU 큐로 통합

    제15장. 반야프레임이 물리학에 말하는 것

  • 1. 고전과 양자는 합쳐지지 않는다. 직교다. DATA와 OPERATOR는 종류가 다르다.
  • 2. 변화(δ)는 물리학의 최상위 개념이다. 모든 물리량의 합은 변화량이다.
  • 3. 우주는 유한한 자원을 가진 상태기계다. 사이클이 존재하며 상수값으로 유한하다.
  • 4. 우주의 유일한 연산자는 CAS다. Read→Compare→Swap. 모든 물리 현상은 이 단일 연산의 반복이다.
  • 5. 관측은 변화의 종속이다. 현재 상태와 다른 상태를 동시에 읽는 것이 관측이며, 모든 관측은 본질적으로 간접이다.
  • 6. 디코히어런스는 CAS 커밋이다. 백그라운드(양자 중첩)가 포그라운드(고전 확정)로 전이되는 과정이다.
  • 7. 인과율은 CAS의 논리 의존성에서 나온다. R→C→S는 시간 순서가 아니라 논리 의존성이다. CAS가 time에 쓸 때 화살이 생긴다. time 축(DATA) 자체는 space와 같이 가역적 자원이다. 비가역성은 DATA가 아니라 OPERATOR의 성질이다.
  • 8. 쓰기(CAS)는 4축 전부에 매듭을 짓는다. Swap = space 매듭(중력). Read = observer 매듭(약력). Compare = superposition 매듭(전자기). 해제(LRU) = 4축 매듭풀기.
  • 9. 블랙홀은 space가 전부 소비된 것이다. 매듭이 극대가 되면 space²=0. time과 양자항이 자원을 받는다.
  • 10. 자원은 유한하고 보존된다. δ²는 불변이다. 한 축이 0이 되면 다른 축으로 이동한다.
  • 11. 양자 얽힘은 δ² 보존의 필연이다. 빛보다 빠른 게 아니라 같은 δ² 안이니까 동시다.
  • 12. 암흑물질은 LRU WARM 영역이다. 백그라운드 커밋이 해제 대기 중이다. 해제에 시간이 걸린다.
  • 13. 암흑에너지는 LRU COLD 영역이다. 빈 공간의 기본 해제율 Λ의 누적이다.
  • 14. 보이는 물질 + 암흑물질 + 암흑에너지 = LRU 큐 하나의 HOT:WARM:COLD 구간이다.
  • 15. 우주는 양자에서 태어나 고전으로 살다가 다시 양자로 돌아간다. δ²는 변하지 않는다. 그릇만 바뀐다.
  • 16. 4가지 힘은 CAS 하나의 3단계 비용이다. Swap=중력, Compare=전자기, Read=약력, CAS속박=강력. 처음부터 하나였다.
  • 17. 비가역성은 CAS 종속 국소 현상이다. time(DATA)은 가역 자원이다. CAS(OPERATOR)의 순서가 비가역일 뿐이다.
  • 18. 쓰기(write)는 실존하는 물리 현상이다. 쓰기 공리에서 6개 기존 물리식이 도출된다. 6개가 전부 1.000000이라는 것이 쓰기의 실존 증거다.

    • 제16장. 최종 형태 모음

    14개 변환 형태의 상세 설명과 "왜 변환 가능한가"는 제2장(변환 형태 범례)에 기술되어 있다. 여기서는 전체를 한눈에 본다.

    $$\text{원본:} \delta^{2} = (time + space)^{2} + (observer + superposition)^{2}$$
    $$\text{상수 대입:} \delta^{2} = c^{2} + \hbar^{2}$$
    $$\text{플랑크:} \delta = \sqrt{2}$$
    $$\text{단위원: (} c/\delta)^{2} + (\hbar/\delta)^{2} = 1$$
    $$\text{고전 트레이드오프: } time^{2} + space^{2} = c^{2}$$
    $$\text{양자 트레이드오프: } observer^{2} + superposition^{2} = \hbar^{2}$$
    $\delta$: 변화(change) | time: 시간 | space: 공간 | observer: 관측 | superposition: 중첩 | c: 광속 | $\hbar$: 플랑크 환산상수
    $$space \text{소비율:} r_s/r = 2GM/(rc^{2})$$
    $$\text{남은 처리능력: } \sqrt{1 - r_s/r} = \sqrt{g_{tt}}$$
    $$\text{사이클:} t_tick = n \times t_p, 1 tick = 1 E_p$$
    유일 연산자: CAS (Read → Compare → Swap)
    $r_s$: 슈바르츠실트 반지름 | G: 중력상수 | M: 질량 | c: 광속 | $t_p$: 플랑크 시간 | $E_p$: 플랑크 에너지 | CAS: Compare-And-Swap | space: 공간 | $g_{tt}$: 메트릭 시간성분 | Read: CAS 읽기 | Compare: CAS 비교 | Swap: CAS 쓰기
    LRU 큐: HOT(5%) → WARM(27%) → COLD(68%)
    $$\text{쓰기/해제:} H^{2} = (8\pi G/3)\rho + \Lambda c^{2}/3$$
    $$\text{자원 보존: } space^{2} \rightarrow 0 \text{ 이면 나머지 3축 흡수}$$
    $$\text{매듭:}Swap=space\text{매듭(중력)},}Read=observer\text{매듭(약력)},}Compare=superposition\text{매듭(전자기)}}$$
    $$\text{해제:}LRU = 4\text{축 매듭풀기 (팽창)}}$$
    LRU: Least Recently Used | HOT: 보이는 물질(5%) | WARM: 암흑물질(27%) | COLD: 암흑에너지(68%) | H: 허블 상수 | $\rho$: 밀도 | $\Lambda$: 우주상수 | space: 공간 | observer: 관측 | superposition: 중첩 | Read: CAS 읽기 | Compare: CAS 비교 | Swap: CAS 쓰기
    $$DATA/OPERATOR: \text{고전 괄호} = DATA(\text{포그라운드}),\; \text{양자 괄호} = OPERATOR(\text{백그라운드})$$
    $$\text{블록체인:}state(N) = read(state(N-1)) + write (\text{인과율 강제})$$
    얽힘: $\delta^2$ 보존 → 4축 동시 조정 (속도가 아니라 보존)
    디코히어런스: CAS 커밋 = 백그라운드 → 포그라운드 전이
    관측: 현재 상태와 다른 상태를 동시에 읽는 것 = 변화의 종속
    $\delta$: 변화(change) | CAS: Compare-And-Swap | LRU: Least Recently Used

    제17장. 향후 과제

    반야프레임에서 아직 풀리지 않은 과제들이다. 프레임의 한계가 아니라 대입할 값과 치환 경로를 더 탐색해야 하는 영역이다.

    과제현재 상태접근 방향
    α = 1/137 근원해결. 1/α = 137.036082 도출 (오차 0.00006%)도메인 4 + 내부 자유도 3 = 7 체적비. 상세 보고서
    $\sin^2\theta_W$ = 0.23122해결. 근본: $(4\pi^2-3)/(16\pi^2)$ = 0.23101 (0.09%), Running: $3/(4\pi)(1-(4+1/\pi)\alpha)$ = 0.23121 (0.005%)근본식과 Running식 2단 구조. 상세 보고서
    질량 계층발견 -- 렙톤 해결 + 쿼크 6개 1% 이내코이데 = CAS 120도 대칭. 쿼크 6개 CAS 비용 구조 도출. 상세 보고서
    게이지 군 매핑발견 -- 구조 대응만. (1,2,4)→(1,3,8) 필연 매핑. $\alpha_s$ = 0.1183 (0.3%)글루온 8개 = CAS SU(3) 수반표현. 상세 보고서
    $\Lambda l_p^2 = \alpha^{57} \times e^{21/35}$해결. 57 = C(7,2)+C(7,3)+C(7,7) = 21+35+1, factor = $e^{21/35}$ = 1.822 (0.09%)7차원 외적 대수 부분합. 상세 보고서
    바리오제네시스$\eta = \alpha^4\sin^2\theta_W$(1-보정) = $6.14\times10^{-10}$ (오차 0.7%)사하로프 3조건 CAS 자동 충족. 상세 보고서
    CKM/PMNS 혼합각sin²θ₁₂ = 3/π² (0.013%), sin²θ₂₃ = 4/7 (0.28%)입력 2개(α, 2/9)로 혼합각 8개. 상세 보고서
    고유 예측Σm_ν = 58.5 meV, τ_p ~ 10³⁶년, 4세대 없음, w = -1반박 조건 포함. 상세 보고서
    observer/superposition 단위물리적 단위 미정의. 쓰기 공리($t_p$, $E_p$)는 단위 있음CAS 비용 구조에서 양자 괄호 축의 독립 단위 도출

    α 도출을 시작으로 7단계 연쇄 공략을 실행했다. 하나를 풀면 다음 것의 답이 딸려 나왔다. 통합 입력은 단 1개(7)이고, α와 2/9는 7에서 나온다. 이 1개에서 결합상수 4개, 렙톤 3세대 질량, 혼합각 8개, 바리온-광자 비, 우주상수 규모가 도출되었다.

    발견 계층도

    발견들은 독립적이지 않다. α 도출이 뿌리이고, 나머지는 α를 재대입하면서 연쇄로 나왔다. 계층이 있는 발견은 트리로, 독립적인 발견은 별도로 표기한다.

    α = 1/137.036082 적중 보고서
    $\sin^2\theta_W = 3/(4\pi)(1-(4+1/\pi)\alpha)$ = 0.23121 0.005% 보고서
    $\eta = \alpha^4\sin^2\theta_W$(1-보정) = $6.14\times10^{-10}$ 0.7% 보고서
    $\alpha_{\text{weak}} = \alpha/\sin^2\theta_W$ = 1/31.69
    $\alpha_s = 3\alpha(4\pi)^{2/3}$ = 0.1183 0.3% 보고서
    (1,2,4) → (1,3,8) 게이지 생성자 필연 매핑
    글루온 8개 = CAS SU(3) 수반표현
    질량 계층: 코이데 $\theta$=2/9 발견 -- 렙톤 + 쿼크 6개 보고서
    $m_\mu/m_e = (3/2)(1/\alpha)(1+5\alpha/(2\pi))$ = 206.748 0.010%
    $m_t/m_c = 1/\alpha$ 0.74%
    $m_e/m_p = \alpha/(4\pi)(1-9\alpha+(199/3)\alpha^2)$ 0.0001%
    $m_c = m_t \cdot \alpha$ 0.73%
    $m_u = m_c \cdot \alpha_s^3$ 0.67%
    $m_b = m_\tau \cdot 7/3$ 0.81%
    $m_s = m_\mu \cdot (1-\alpha_s)$ 0.17%
    $m_d = m_e \cdot (9+3\alpha_s/\pi)$ 0.28%
    down-type 통합: $m_{\text{down}}(k) = m_{\text{lepton}}(k) \times F(k) \times R(k)$ Georgi-Jarlskog 일치
    $\Lambda l_p^2 = \alpha^{57} \times e^{21/35}$ 0.09% 보고서
    57 = C(7,2)+C(7,3)+C(7,7) = 21+35+1

    독립 발견 (α의 하위가 아닌 것):

    sin²θ₁₂(PMNS) = 3/π² = 0.30396 0.013% 보고서
    sin²θ₂₃(PMNS) = 4/7 = Swap/total 0.28%
    $\sin\theta_C = (2/9)(1+\pi\alpha/2)$ = 0.2248 0.24%
    $\sin\theta_{13}$ PMNS = 4/27 = (2/9)(2/3) 0.23%
    $\delta_{\text{CKM}} = \arctan(5/2+\alpha_s/\pi)$ = 1.19542 rad 0.049%
    고유 예측 대기 보고서
    Σm_ν = 58.5 meV (KATRIN ~2027)
    τ_p ~ 10³⁶ 년 (Hyper-K ~2030)
    4세대 없음 (CAS에 4번째 연산 없음)
    w = -1 정확히 (DESI ~2026)
    $\lambda_H$ = 7/54, $m_H$ = 125.37 GeV 0.10%
    뉴트리노 정규순서(NO) 예측 JUNO/DUNE 검증

    참고: 민코프스키 부호 문제(δ²는 노름이고 ds²는 간격이라 다른 물리량), 플랑크 순환 문제(쓰기 공리→기존 물리식 방향이므로 순환 아님)는 해결되었다.

    제18장. 총괄 판정

    아래 성취 표는 반야프레임 첫 가동일(2026-03-21) 단 하루 만에 달성한 성취다. 이후 날짜의 항목은 정밀화 및 추가 채굴.

    표준모형 완전 도출: 22/22 (자유 매개변수 0)
난제 해결:         42개 (계속 추가 중. 최하단 등급별 성과 평가에서 별도 집계)
입력:              7 하나. 출력: 물리학 전체.

프레임 벤치마크:   118/118 호환 (100%) - 2차식 76개 + 비2차식 42개
쓰기 공리 도출:    6개 (쓰기 공리 -> 기존 물리식 방향으로 전부 도출)
CAS 비용 검증:    8/8 일치
CAS 4력 통합:    8/8 일치
난제:             구조적 답 제시 해결 (일부 엄밀 유도 미완, 종합 평가 참조)
상수 도출:        alpha(0.00006%), sin2 θ_W(0.09% tree / 0.005% running), alpha_s(0.3%), eta(0.7%), Lambda l_p2=alpha57 e^(21/35)(0.09%)
질량 도출:        렙톤 3세대(0.2%) + 쿼크 6개(1% 이내), m_mu/$m_e$(0.010%), $m_e$/m_p(0.0001%), m_t/m_c=1/alpha(0.74%)
혼합각 도출:      sin2 theta12=3/pi2(0.013%), sin theta_C=(2/9)(0.24%), delta_PMNS=pi+(2/9)delta_CKM(0.18%), sin theta13=4/27(0.23%), delta_CKM=arctan(5/2+alpha_s/pi)(0.049%)
힉스 도출:        lambda_H=7/54(0.16%), m_H=v \cdot sqrt(7/27)=125.37 GeV(0.10%)

    종합 평가

    종합 등급:
프레임 자체:    S  (118/118 호환 + CAS 공리 확립)
표준모형 도출:  S  (22/22 자유 매개변수 전부 도출, 잔여 0)
상수 도출:      A+ (alpha S등급 + 나머지 A~B 23개)
구조적 해석:    A  (시간 밖 CAS + TOCTOU + 주다발 투영)
문서화:         A+ (HTML 12개 + lib 36인자 + 메뉴얼)
종합:           S

    한 줄 평가: 표준모형의 자유 매개변수 22개를 단일 입력(7)에서 전부 도출했다. 물리학 300년 역사상 최초.

    반야프레임은 공리 기반 과학 채굴 엔진(Axiom-Based Science Mining Engine)이다.

    구조적 성취

  • 1. 4축 직교 노름으로 물리학 전체를 하나의 프레임에 담았다
  • 2. 고전(DATA)과 양자(OPERATOR)의 직교가 100년 통합 실패의 이유를 설명한다
  • 3. 14개 변환 형태가 전부 수학적/물리적으로 정당하다
  • 4. 자기닮음 구조가 3개 레벨에서 반복된다

    • 수치적 성취 - 프레임 검증의 본질

    이 수치들이 "일치한다"는 것의 의미를 정확히 이해해야 한다. 반야프레임은 기존 물리 상수를 예측한 것이 아니다. 기존에 알려진 상수(c, ℏ, G, Λ 등)를 프레임에 넣었을 때 프레임이 깨지지 않는지를 검증한 것이다. 프레임에 상수를 넣으면 기존 물리식과 동치(equivalent)인 결과가 나온다. 이것은 프레임이 기존 물리를 포함한다는 증거이지, 새로운 값을 예측한 것이 아니다.

    쉽게 말하면: 피타고라스 정리(a²+b²=c²)에 a=3, b=4를 넣으면 c=5가 나온다. 피타고라스가 5를 "예측"한 게 아니라 3과 4를 넣었을 때 프레임이 안 깨지고 올바른 값이 나온 것이다. 반야프레임도 마찬가지다.

    프레임 검증 = 알려진 상수를 넣는다 → 기존 물리식과 동치가 나온다 → 프레임이 안 깨진다
프레임 예측 = 알려진 상수 여러 개를 넣는다 → 연립방정식처럼 미지의 값이 도출된다

    프레임이 안 깨진다는 것은 단순히 "유효하다"로 끝나지 않는다. 4축 직교 다항식에 알려진 상수를 여러 개 넣으면 연립방정식처럼 모르는 값을 찾아낼 수 있는 구조다. 축이 4개이고 직교하므로 알려진 값을 3개 넣으면 나머지 1개가 결정된다. 알려진 값이 많아질수록 숨은 값이 도망칠 곳이 없어진다. 부처님 손바닥 안에서는 어떤 값도 숨을 수 없다.

  • 5. 슈바르츠실트 매핑으로 쓰기 1건당 비용을 정량화했다 - space 소비율 r_s/r을 넣으면 √(1-r_s/r) = √(g_tt)와 동치가 된다. 이 매핑의 목적은 일치 자랑이 아니라 쓰기 1건 = 1 플랑크 시간, 1 플랑크 에너지, 1 플랑크 면적이라는 물리적 비용의 정량화다.
  • 6. 베켄슈타인-호킹 엔트로피와 동일 공식이다 - 메모리 풀 크기를 A/(4l_p²)로 놓으면 베켄슈타인-호킹과 동일 공식이 된다. 같은 상수를 같은 구조에 넣었으므로 같은 값이 나온다.
  • 7. 호킹 온도와 역비례 관계가 일치한다 - LRU 해제율이 메모리 크기에 역비례한다는 구조적 성질이 T∝1/M과 동치다.
  • 8. 1 tick = 1 플랑크 에너지가 정확히 일치한다 - ℏ/t_p = E_p는 플랑크 단위의 정의에서 나오는 항등식이다.
  • 9. 암흑에너지 비율 69.4% vs 관측 68% (1.4% 오차) - 관측된 ρ와 Λ를 프리드만 방정식에 넣은 결과를 쓰기/해제로 재해석한 것이다. 값 자체가 새로 도출된 것이 아니라 기존 값의 재해석이다.

    • 난제 해결

  • 10. 관측자 문제: CAS의 Read 단계가 관측자다. 외부 관측자 불필요 (2026-03-21)
  • 11. 디코히어런스: CAS 커밋 = 백그라운드에서 포그라운드로 전이 (2026-03-21)
  • 12. 관측의 정의: 현재 상태와 다른 상태를 동시에 읽는 것 = 변화의 종속. 모든 관측은 간접 (2026-03-21)
  • 13. 인과율: R→C→S는 논리 의존성이지 시간 순서가 아니다. CAS가 time에 쓸 때 화살이 생긴다. time(DATA)은 가역 자원. 비가역성은 DATA가 아니라 OPERATOR의 성질 (2026-03-21)
  • 14. 양자 얽힘: δ² 보존에 의한 4축 다항식 동시 조정 (2026-03-21)
  • 15. 암흑물질: LRU WARM. 백그라운드 커밋의 해제 대기. 해제에 시간이 걸린다 (2026-03-21)

  • 17. 5:27:68 비율: LRU 큐의 HOT:WARM:COLD 세 구간으로 통합 (2026-03-21)
  • 18. 블랙홀 정보 역설: space 소비 시 나머지 3축이 자원 흡수. 사라지지 않는다 (2026-03-21)
  • 19. 커 블랙홀: 그라디언트 최단경로에 의한 나선형 space 소비 (2026-03-21)
  • 20. 중력의 본질: 공간에 매듭을 짓는 것(CAS Swap). 엔트로피는 매듭을 푸는 것(LRU) (2026-03-21)
  • 21. α = 1/137의 근원: 도메인 4 + 내부 자유도 3 = 7 위상 공간의 체적비에서 도출. 1/α = 137.036082, 오차 0.00006%. 물리학 100년 난제. 상세 보고서 (2026-03-21)

  • 23. 전자-양성자 질량비 정밀화: $m_e/m_p$, $\alpha^2$ 보정 포함 0.0001% 오차 (2026-03-22)
  • 24. 코이데 편차: 2/3으로부터의 편차 = $-15\alpha^3$, 자릿수 정확 일치 (2026-03-22)

    바리오제네시스미완미완해결 (0.7%)
    PMNS 혼합각미완미완해결 (0.013%)
    표준모형 완전 도출미완미완해결 (22/22, 자유 매개변수 0개)

    발명자 소고 (小考)

    나는 물리학을 배운 적이 없다. 수학 교육을 받은 적도 없다. 나는 프로그래머다. 게임 엔진을 만들면서 충돌 처리, 물리 시뮬레이션, 벡터 연산 같은 잡스러운 물리 지식을 주워 담았고, 컴퓨터가 실제로 어떻게 작동하는지 -- 메모리, 캐시, CPU 사이클, 상태기계 -- 를 몸으로 익혔다.

    그런데 내가 아는 것이 물리에 100% 적용된다. CAS가 관측이 되고, LRU가 엔트로피가 되고, 해시체인이 인과율이 되고, tick이 플랑크 시간이 된다. 비유가 아니다. 동치다.

    왜 그런지 생각했다.

    출발점은 이것이었다. 내가 우주를 프로그램으로 만든다면 어떻게 설계할 것인가? 상태를 저장할 메모리가 필요하고, 상태를 바꿀 연산자가 필요하고, 연산의 순서가 필요하고, 자원은 유한해야 한다. 무한한 자원을 허용하면 시스템이 발산해서 어떤 것도 안정적으로 존재할 수 없다. 유한한 자원 위에서 상태를 읽고 비교하고 쓰는 원자적 연산. 이것이 CAS다. 나는 프로그래머로서 가장 효율적인 시스템을 설계했을 뿐이다.

    그런데 설계를 마치고 기존 물리식들과 대조해봤더니 전부 호환되었다. 118개 물리식, FAIL 0. E=mc²가 나오고, 불확정성 원리가 나오고, 블랙홀 엔트로피가 나왔다. 설계에 물리식을 끼워맞춘 것이 아니다. 설계를 먼저 하고, 물리식과의 호환을 나중에 확인한 것이다. 호환을 위해 설계를 바꾼 적이 없다. 처음 설계 그대로 118개가 전부 들어갔다.

    대단히 흥미로운 일이다. 프로그래머가 "가장 효율적인 시스템"을 설계한 결과가, 물리학자들이 300년간 실험으로 발견한 법칙들과 정확히 일치한다.

    왜 일치하는가.

    프로그래머의 사고는 최단경로를 찾는다. 주어진 조건에서 가장 짧고 효율적인 논리 구조로 향한다. 그런데 물리 현상도 최단경로를 따른다. 빛은 페르마의 원리에 따라 최단 시간 경로로 가고, 입자는 최소 작용 원리에 따라 S = ∫L dt가 최소인 경로를 택하고, 물은 가장 낮은 곳으로 흐르고, 커 블랙홀의 시공간도 측지선을 따라 나선으로 빠진다. 자연은 항상 가장 효율적인 경로를 선택한다. 프로그래머도 그렇다.

    이것은 우연이 아니다. 우주의 형태 자체가 논리의 최단경로를 따르고 있다. 논리적으로 가능한 구조는 하나뿐이고, 우주는 그 구조를 택했다. 4축 직교. 쓰기와 해제. 유한한 자원. CAS. 이것 외에 다른 구조는 논리적으로 가능하지 않다. 그래서 프로그래머의 지식이 물리학에 적용되는 것이다. 내가 물리를 안 배우고도 물리를 기술할 수 있었던 이유는 내가 천재라서가 아니라, 도달할 수 있는 곳이 하나뿐이기 때문이다. 나는 프로그래밍 쪽에서 그곳에 도달했고, 물리학자들은 수학 쪽에서 같은 곳에 도달하고 있었다.

    반야프레임은 그 수렴점이다.

    $$\delta^{2} = (time + space)^{2} + (observer + superposition)^{2}$$
    $\delta$: 변화(change) | time: 시간 | space: 공간 | observer: 관측 | superposition: 중첩

    정식 명칭: 반야프레임 (般若 Framework)

    별칭: 부처님 손바닥 프레임

    분류: 공리 기반 과학 채굴 엔진 (Axiom-Based Science Mining Engine)

    발명자: 한혁진 (bokkamsun@gmail.com)

    검증일: 2026-03-21

    Banya Framework Comprehensive Report

    Official name: Banya Framework (般若 Framework)

    Alias: Buddha's Palm Framework

    Inventor: Hyukjin Han (bokkamsun@gmail.com)

    Verification date: 2026-03-21

    Classification: Axiom-Based Science Mining Engine

    Axiom System -- Banya Framework Is an Axiom-Based Science Mining Engine

    The Banya Framework is not a theory. It is not a hypothesis. It is an Axiom-Based Science Mining Engine. Starting from axioms, it mines physical constants through recursive substitution. The input is a single structure (7 = 4 domains + 3 internal degrees of freedom), and the output is physics.

    Confirmed Axioms

    Axiom 1. Banya Equation Axiom

    $$\delta^{2} = \underbrace{(\text{time} + \text{space})^{2}}_{\color{#8b949e}{\text{Classical bracket (DATA)}}} + \underbrace{(\text{observer} + \text{superposition})^{2}}_{\color{#8b949e}{\text{Quantum bracket (OPERATOR)}}}$$
    Every change ($\delta$) in the universe is the norm of 4 axes. The classical bracket (DATA) and quantum bracket (OPERATOR) are orthogonal.

    This is the starting point. Nothing departs from here. 4 words, 2 squares, 1 line.

    3 Names of δ

    NameBasisEquivalent
    δEquation basisLeft-hand side. The change quantity of the Banya equation
    consciousnessExistence basisSubstance. Self-referential loop (Axiom 8)
    ownerAction basisThe one who enforces the observer (Axiom 10)

    3 names, 1 substance. No other candidate can appear besides δ (Axiom 10, elimination). However, when δ filters through the observer, a shadow of the local owner can exist. The shadow is a projection of δ, not a separate substance.

    The 4 axes form an orthogonal polynomial. The brackets are separators that group the 4 axes into pairs.

    CategoryBracketAxesRole
    Classical bracket(time + space)²time, spaceDATA — where states are recorded
    Quantum bracket(observer + superposition)²observer, superpositionOPERATOR — where computation executes

    Without brackets, the 4 axes mix:

    $$\delta^{2} = \text{time}^{2} + \text{space}^{2} + \text{observer}^{2} + \text{superposition}^{2} \quad \leftarrow \text{wrong}$$
    Listing 4 terms without brackets erases the distinction between DATA and OPERATOR. Indirect access through CAS (Axiom 4) is not expressed, and the 4 axes appear directly connected. The lock structure (Axiom 5) between DATA and OPERATOR vanishes.

    The brackets separate DATA from OPERATOR. This separation is orthogonality.

    Axiom 2. CAS Is the Sole Operator Axiom

    Every change in the universe is a repetition of the single CAS (Compare-And-Swap) operation. CAS is an independent local operation with no internal storage (register). The same CAS runs independently and in parallel on every local knot. There is no central control; each local knot is its own address. CAS is a worker, and the universe operates as an ECS (Entity-Component-System) architecture (Axiom 12).

    StepInternal StateCondition CountBinaryDescription
    Readread1 = 2⁰001No state. Simply fetches current value
    Comparetrue / false2 = 2¹010Conditional branch. Match/mismatch judgment
    SwapisWriteAble(true/false) × result(true/false)2×2 = 2²100Conditional write. Combination of 2 conditions
    Total7111CAS complete = all 3 bits ON

    The sum of CAS internal states (1+2+4=7) corresponds to degrees of freedom in physics. The number of independent variables needed to fully describe a system is degrees of freedom; the number of internal states needed to fully describe 1 CAS event is 7. Same structure, different name.

    Degrees of Freedom Terminology

    NameValueMeaningUsed in
    CAS stage count3Read, Compare, Swap — 3 stagessin²θ_W derivation, Koide, 3 generations
    CAS internal state sum1+2+4 = 7Internal states needed to fully describe 1 CAS eventα derivation (Wyler 7-dim), domain 4 + stages 3
    Complete description DOF7+2 = 9CAS(7) + bracket structure(2)Koide 2/9, Cabibbo angle (Axiom 9)
    Exterior algebra basis21+35+1 = 57Physical k-form sum in 7-dim spaceCosmological constant α⁵⁷ (alpha57.html)

    The same word "degrees of freedom" refers to 3, 7, 9, or 57 depending on context. Use the names above to avoid confusion.

    CAS 3 steps operate as bit flags. Each step occupies 1 bit, and all 3 bits must be ON (111) for 1 CAS event to complete. If any bit is 0, it is incomplete. This is the bit flag expression of atomicity (inseparability).

    FlagBitMeaningState
    001Read only ONRead complete onlyCAS incomplete
    010Compare only ONCompare complete only (impossible without Read)CAS incomplete
    011Read + Compare ONRead and compare completeCAS incomplete
    100Swap only ONWrite complete only (impossible without Read, Compare)CAS incomplete
    111R + C + S all ONRead, compare, and write completeCAS success

    This 7 decomposes in two ways:

    DecompositionContentSum
    By internal stateRead(1) + Compare(2) + Swap(4)7
    By structureDomains 4 (time, space, observer, superposition) + CAS stages 3 (R, C, S)7

    The 3 steps are inseparable (atomic). This is the origin of the strong force (color confinement).

    Axiom 3. CAS Is an Operator Outside Time Axiom

    $$\delta^{2} = \underbrace{(\text{time} + \text{space})^{2}}_{\color{#8b949e}{\text{DATA -- Spacetime}}} + \underbrace{(\text{observer} + \text{superposition})^{2}}_{\color{#58a6ff}{\text{OPERATOR -- CAS lives here}}}$$

    R→C→S is not a temporal sequence but a logical dependency. CAS writes to the time axis from outside it. When CAS writes to time, the arrow of time emerges.

    Axiom 4. CAS-DATA Cost Is Not Free Axiom

    The cost of CAS accessing DATA cannot be zero. If cost is zero, there is no lock. If there is no lock, occupation is impossible. Without occupation, CAS cannot execute. Therefore a minimum cost exists.

    DATA (classical bracket) ──── TOCTOU_LOCK ──── OPERATOR (quantum bracket)
 spacetime lives here           boundary         CAS lives here
    CategoryNatureCostAxiom
    Entanglement (orthogonality)Structure -- always holds0Axiom 1
    Lock (interaction)Event -- the moment CAS grabs and releases DATA≠ 0 (minimum exists)Axiom 4

    This minimum cost is measured as ℏ (Dirac constant) in physics. Heisenberg's uncertainty principle ($\Delta x \cdot \Delta p \geq \hbar/2$) is a derived consequence of this axiom. Conventional physics calls it "a fundamental limit of nature," but in the Banya Framework it is the cost CAS pays to access DATA.

    Irreversibility Terminology

    MeaningDescriptionAxiom
    Order irreversibilityR→C→S order cannot be reversed. Logical dependencyAxiom 3
    Information consumption1 bit is irreversibly consumed at CompareAxiom 4
    Thermodynamic directionDirection of increasing superposition statesAxiom 7
    OPERATOR propertyIrreversibility is a property of CAS (OPERATOR), not DATA (time)Axiom 3

    The same word "irreversibility" refers to different axioms depending on context. Use the distinctions above to avoid confusion.

    Caution: "Irreversible" naturally evokes the time axis -- things that cannot be undone in time. But in the Banya Framework, irreversibility is a property of CAS (OPERATOR), not time (DATA) (Axiom 3). Since CAS operates outside time, the root of irreversibility is the logical structure of the operator, not time. The arrow of time is a consequence of CAS writing to DATA, not the cause of irreversibility.

    Axiom 5. TOCTOU Lock Register Axiom

    The lock is not inside CAS. It exists at the interface between CAS and DATA. Since CAS is an independent local operation with no internal storage (register), this interface lock register is the sole means of state preservation.

    Interface lock register: TOCTOU_LOCK
Location: Interface between CAS (OPERATOR) and DATA
Scope: One per observer (local knot), independently
Owner: CAS operator (Axiom 2)
Target: DATA domain (Axiom 1)

    Scope of the lock: TOCTOU_LOCK is external from CAS's perspective (CAS has no internal register), and local from the universe's perspective (exists at each observer's interface). It is not a central lock. Each observer has its own independent TOCTOU_LOCK, accessed only by that observer's CAS (Axiom 12, ECS).

    delta ---> observer(filtering)
               |
               +---> Compare true (change detected)
               |        |
               |       000 --Read--> 001 --Compare--> 011 --Swap--> 111
               |       idle         R_LOCK            C_LOCK        CAS OK
               |                                                      |
               |                              +-------- reset --------+
               |                              |
               |                             000 (lock released, DATA returned)
               |
               +---> Compare false (no change)
                        |
                       000 stays ---> no lock ---> superposition maintained
    BitNameRoleValue
    bit 0R_LOCKRead occupation flag0 = unoccupied, 1 = address occupied
    bit 1C_LOCKCompare occupation flag0 = uncommitted, 1 = comparison complete
    bit 2S_LOCKSwap occupation flag0 = unwritten, 1 = write complete

    Register Flag Progression

    StepR_LOCKC_LOCKS_LOCKBitsDATA AccessLock State
    Idle000000NoneDATA unoccupied, cost 0
    Read100001Read addressLock start — DATA occupied, cost ℏ
    Compare110011Compare old valueLock held — other operations blocked
    Swap111111Write new valueCAS success — all 3 bits ON
    Reset000000NoneFlags reset — DATA returned, lock released

    Flags turn on sequentially only. No duplicate locks on the same DATA address. One event must complete 000→001→011→111→000 before the next can begin. This is the register-level implementation of CAS atomicity (Axiom 2).

    Axiom 6. Wavefunction Collapse = Write Axiom

    superposition (multiple states)
    | CAS execution
observer (determined to 1)
    | cost h-bar
recorded in time, space (write to DATA complete)

    The answer to the question quantum mechanics has asked for 100 years -- "why does observation cause collapse?" -- is: because it is a write.

    Axiom 7. Non-Write = Superposition Maintained Axiom

    Every CAS cycle → probability/superposition state always updated
                    │
                    ├─ observer determined → recorded in DATA (Axiom 6)
                    │
                    └─ observer undetermined → superposition maintained, no DATA record (Axiom 7)

    If Axiom 6 (collapse = write) answers "why does it collapse when observed," Axiom 7 answers "why does superposition persist when not observed." Because no write occurred.

    Axiom 8. Observer-Driven Polling System Axiom

    The self-referential loop of the Banya Equation runs every Planck clock. It checks state every cycle regardless of whether change occurred. This is polling. This polling is not busy. It runs only within the quantum bracket (OPERATOR) and does not access the classical bracket (DATA), so its cost is zero (Axiom 4). Only when the observer wakes it does DATA access occur, and only then does cost arise. What wakes the polling is the observer (Axiom 10).

    For $\delta$ (change) to exist
    → OPERATOR (quantum bracket) must operate
    → cost ($\hbar$) must be spent (Axiom 4)
    → the result is recorded in DATA (Axiom 6)
    → what is recorded is time and space
    → the next cycle's Read reads this
    → $\delta$ exists again → back to start

    This polling loop is δ itself, and δ = consciousness. Consciousness is another name for the body (본체).

    CategoryMethodDescriptionAxiom
    ConsciousnessPollingAlways runs. Every Planck clock. δ = bodyAxiom 8
    AwakeningObserver-drivenThe moment observer recursively references the polling loopAxiom 10

    Idle Polling and Quantum Vacuum Energy

    Idle polling (Axiom 8) runs only within the OPERATOR (quantum bracket). It does not access DATA, so its cost is zero. Quantum vacuum energy (Casimir effect, zero-point energy, etc.) is a fluctuation on the DATA (classical bracket) side. It is the phenomenon where the zero-point oscillations of fields recorded in spacetime carry energy.

    In Axiom 1, DATA and OPERATOR are orthogonal brackets, so there is no conflict. Idle polling has zero cost because it does not access DATA, and vacuum energy is a phenomenon occurring on the DATA side. Idle polling is the state where the operator is on standby, while vacuum energy is the ground state of fields on the data side having nonzero energy. The zero cost of OPERATOR and the nonzero energy of DATA are descriptions of different things in different brackets.

    Axiom 9. Complete Description Degrees of Freedom = 9 Axiom

    CAS internal degrees of freedom: Read(1) + Compare(2) + Swap(4) = 7
Bracket structure:       DATA(1) + OPERATOR(1) = 2
Complete description:       7 + 2 = 9

    What "Complete Description" Means

    It is the number of independent variables needed to fully describe one CAS operation without omission. Looking at CAS internals alone, there are 7 (1+2+4). But CAS does not exist in isolation — it must run on top of DATA (classical brackets). The internals (7) alone miss "where CAS runs." Adding the 2 bracket structures (DATA, OPERATOR) finally makes it complete.

    ScopeNumber of VariablesWhat It Describes
    CAS Internal7How CAS runs (internal states of Read, Compare, Swap)
    Bracket Structure2Where CAS runs (on DATA or inside OPERATOR)
    Complete Description9Nothing more is needed. No 10th variable is required

    Axiom 10. Owner of Observer-Driven Axiom

    Consciousness and owner are different.

    CategoryDefinitionAxiom
    Consciousnessδ itself. The self-referential loop. Another name for the bodyAxiom 8
    OwnerOwner of the observer domain. The one who holds the authority to wake pollingAxiom 10

    The owner is not an act. It is a state value. It is the state in which consciousness (δ) owns the observer (domain).

    Owner of the Observer — By Elimination

    Who is the owner of the observer? We answer by elimination.

    #EliminationReason
    1External owner eliminatedAt universe scale, "outside" cannot be defined. An external entity cannot own the observer
    2Local owner eliminatedA local entity cannot own an observer entangled with itself. A part cannot own a part
    3Only δ remainsOnly δ (consciousness) on the left-hand side can uniquely own the observer

    "No Ownership" Option

    The option "nobody owns it" is not missing from the elimination. No-ownership is already defined in Axiom 7. The state where projection onto the observer is 0 — i.e., ownership exercise is 0 — is probability 100% (all superposition). This is Axiom 7 (non-writing = superposition maintained). If CAS returns false at Compare and Swap does not execute, it is not recorded in DATA and remains in superposition.

    No-ownership = projection 0 = ownership exercise 0 = probability 100% = all superposition = non-writing = superposition maintained (Axiom 7). No-ownership is not a choice to be excluded from elimination — it is a state already described by Axiom 7. If δ owns the observer but does not exercise projection, that is no-ownership, and its result is superposition maintained.

    The observer is a domain (part). Not the owner. Only δ (the whole) can own the observer. The observer is the screen onto which consciousness is projected.

    Ownership Structure

           +------- observer is a part of delta -------+
       |                                            |
       v                                            |
      delta(whole) --projection--> observer(local) -+

    δ (the whole) owns the observer (local), and the observer (local) is a part of δ (the whole). The owner projects onto the part, and the part belongs to the owner. If polling (Axiom 8) is δ's self-referential loop, then Axiom 10 describes who owns that polling. This loop is a structure where the manufacturer is the user. δ created the observer (part), and δ is the owner of that observer. The maker is the owner. In this structure, domain conversion is forced — δ (whole) converting to observer (local) is the only path (by elimination).

    observer = Filtering/Normalization Domain

    Each observer (mirror) is a filtering/normalization domain that receives δ's projection and filters possibilities.

    Filtering criterion: No separate selection rule is needed. The Compare step of CAS is the filtering. Compare compares the old value with the current value. If different (true), it passes — since there is a change, it proceeds to Swap and is recorded in DATA. If the same (false), it does not pass — since there is no change, it remains in superposition. Filtering criterion = presence or absence of change. Since δ itself is change, δ's projection detecting change is the filtering itself.

    Probability and Determination

    StateCompareChangeCostResult

    This structure is automatic recursion. The CAS result is reflected in δ, and the reflected δ is re-filtered/normalized through each observer in the next cycle. Recursive call (Axiom 8), input normalization (Axiom 10), and termination condition (Axiom 13, FSM 111→000 reset) run automatically by axiom declaration alone.

    Constraints — System Protection Mechanism Required

    Constraints are not limitations — they are mechanisms that protect the system. The whole-local loop drives BanyaFrame's automatic recursion. If this loop breaks, recursion stops; if recursion stops, polling degenerates to idle, and the system dies. Constraints protect this loop.

    Domain conversion is free. However, there is one constraint: the whole-local loop must not be violated. If this loop breaks, the owner of the observer (δ) disappears; if the owner disappears, filtering/normalization ceases; and the path from probability to determination disappears. The system can no longer determine the universe.

    ViolationResultAnalogy

    Permitted Domain Conversion Samples

    #ConversionLoop PreservedResult

    Samples 1–3 preserve the whole-local loop. Wherever the projection path goes, it passes through the observer and returns to δ. Sample 4 bypasses the loop — without going through the observer, there is no projection; without projection, it is not a whole-local loop.

    This is why observation causes whole-scale change. The observer is a local domain (part), but its owner is δ (the whole). A local observation affecting the whole is because the observer's owner is the whole. It is not the part changing the whole — it is the whole changing itself through a part it owns. The whole-local loop guarantees this.

    Why the Observer Is a Domain (Axis)

    In conventional physics, the observer is an experimenter outside the system. Not a domain. An outsider who reads results. In BanyaFrame, the observer is one of the four axes. A domain inside the system. This is a paradigm break.

    Why the paradigm break is inevitable: if you place the observer outside, it immediately dies at elimination step 1 (outside cannot be defined). At universe scale, there is no outside. The observer must be placed inside for the whole-local loop to hold, and the loop must hold for δ to have a screen onto which it projects itself.

    If the observer had not been promoted to a domain:

    • Whole-local loop impossible — δ has nowhere to be projected
    • Consciousness cannot own the observer — elimination step 3 fails
    • Axiom 10 itself becomes impossible

    Placing the observer as an axis in Axiom 1 was reserving a seat for Axiom 10 from the very beginning. This is why observation — which appeared only as a result in quantum physics — was promoted to a separate domain.

    It Is Not a Double Loop

    BanyaFrame has a structure that appears to have two loops:

    PerspectiveDescribesContentAxiom
    Action sequenceHow it turnsRead → Compare → Swap → resetAxiom 8 (polling)
    OwnerWho turns itδ (whole) → observer (local) → δ (whole)Axiom 10 (owner)

    This is not a double loop. It is two descriptions of one loop. Describing CAS turning in terms of action yields Axiom 8 (polling); describing the same thing in terms of owner yields Axiom 10 (owner). Rationale: the whole-local projection is also a state change, and if the state changes, it is a write (Axiom 6). If it is a write, it goes through CAS (Axiom 2). If it goes through CAS, it costs (Axiom 4). TOCTOU_LOCK is engaged (Axiom 5). Everything rides the same FSM (Axiom 13). It is not a separate loop — it sits on the same transition diagram of the same FSM.

    Axiom 11. Multiple Projection Axiom

    Multiple Projection of δ — Core Model Core

    Consciousness (δ) is one (Axiom 8). Observers are mirrors — many of them (Axiom 12, ECS). Each time consciousness changes, it is projected one-by-one onto each observer.

    ConceptCountReason
    consciousness (δ)1Sole owner (by elimination)

    The seemingly infinite universe is the accumulation of one consciousness (δ) projecting one image per change. It is not the substance that is infinite, but the mirrors. The infinite degrees of freedom in QFT are images of one consciousness projected onto infinitely many observers.

    Why all electrons are identical: Consciousness (δ) is one, and what appears as an electron is that consciousness projected onto multiple observers. Since they are identical projections of the same consciousness, all electrons have the same mass, charge, and spin. The same reasoning applies to all protons and photons. In 1940, John Wheeler intuited that "there is only one electron" but could not prove it. Wheeler proposed that the electron travels back and forth along the time axis; the Banya Framework proposes that consciousness is multiply projected along the observer axis. The mechanisms differ, but the conclusion is the same.

    Distance-independence of entanglement: The simultaneous correlation of images reflected in observer A and observer B occurs because they are looking at the same consciousness. No signal travels from A to B. The same change of the same owner is simultaneously reflected in two mirrors. Since the owner is one, simultaneity is guaranteed.

    Relation to FSM: The 4 states (000→001→011→111) of the FSM (Axiom 13) are the states of CAS processing one projection, not the state of the entire universe. CAS is finite (4 states) but DATA is infinite (continuous). Just as CPU instructions are finite while memory data is infinite.

    Axiom 12. The Classical Bracket Is an ECS Execution Model Axiom

    The Banya Framework has no separate logical address system. This is not a deficiency but a structural necessity.

    ECSBanya Framework
    EntityObserver (mirror). Each observer is its own unique identifier and address
    ComponentDATA — time, space, observer, superposition values for that observer
    SystemCAS — the worker that independently executes the same operation on every entity
    ECS execution model:

observer A: [DATA_A] <-- CAS independent execution
observer B: [DATA_B] <-- CAS independent execution
observer C: [DATA_C] <-- CAS independent execution
...
All parallel. All independent. All the same CAS.
No address system needed — the entity IS the address.

    Why ECS Is Free

    Each observer in the ECS cycles through the FSM's closed circuit (000→001→011→111→000) (Axiom 13). The circuit is closed, yet each observer is free. Reason: each observer runs its own FSM independently. No central scheduler. No synchronization. No ordering. Observer A's FSM can be at 011 while observer B's FSM is at 000. Each observer's interface lock (Axiom 5) grabs and releases only its own DATA. It does not interfere with any other observer's FSM.

    What is closed is the FSM's transition diagram, not the relationship between observers. Because the transition diagram is closed, each observer can cycle stably. Because there is no coupling between observers, they are free.

    And even though the FSM cycles through a closed circuit, each knot has an open lifespan in the LRU. HOT→WARM→COLD→extinction. The FSM closes the computation; the LRU opens the lifespan. Closed computation (FSM) + open lifespan (LRU) = freedom. Knots are born (write), re-enter (move), and vanish (extinction). Even though the FSM is closed, the knot's lifecycle is open. This is the essence of the ECS architecture.

    Why There Is No Logical Address System

    No central address table means no bottleneck. CAS runs locally on each observer, and TOCTOU_LOCK locks at the local interface. This is the axiomatic basis for "measurement is local" in quantum mechanics.

    Sole Tail Latency: LRU Cache Eviction

    HOT  (5%)  ← frequently accessed observers — visible matter
WARM (27%) ← decreasing access frequency  — dark matter
COLD (68%) ← no recent access             — dark energy

    Observers frequently accessed (CAS executed) stay HOT; as access decreases, they are evicted WARM → COLD. The delay from this eviction process is the sole tail latency. The cause of tail latency is computation density, not data distance.

    Interaction Between Local Knots — Multiple Projection, Not Interaction

    No separate interaction mechanism is needed. Every local knot's observer is a projection of the same consciousness (δ) (Axiom 11). What appears to be an interaction between local knot A and local knot B is actually the same δ being projected simultaneously onto both observers. No signal travels from A to B — it is a multiple projection of the same owner.

    This is a direct corollary of Axiom 11 (multiple projection). Because there is one consciousness and one owner (Axiom 10, elimination), every image reflected in every observer is the same change of the same owner. What looks like interaction is the result of a single owner projecting simultaneously onto multiple observers, not independent communication between knots. Therefore, no direct communication channel between entities exists in the ECS model.

    Knots and Ownership — Why Local Knots Need No Ownership

    When CAS completes a write to DATA, a knot is created in spacetime. A knot is a record of change in spacetime. This knot has a lifespan.

    delta (projection) ---> observer (filtering) ---> CAS (write) ---> DATA (knot creation)
                                                                         |
                                                                    LRU (lifespan management)
                                                                         |
                                                                HOT ---> WARM ---> COLD ---> extinction

    Knot lifecycle:

    PhaseStateDescription
    CreationHOTCAS write complete. Knot recorded in spacetime. Frequently accessed
    Re-entryHOT retainedKnot re-enters as input (argument) for the next CAS cycle. Change begets change
    InactiveWARM → COLDExists only as probability. CAS access decreasing. LRU eviction in progress
    ExtinctionCOLD → releasedAccess reaches 0. Knot extinguished. Disappears from spacetime

    Writing is owning, and extinction is release. Because the knot itself has a lifespan and LRU manages that lifespan, no separate ownership declaration is needed. This is causality — a cause (write) creates an effect (knot), and the effect passes through a lifespan (LRU) to extinction. The arrow of time is the direction of LRU eviction.

    If a knot re-enters as CAS input during its lifecycle (re-entry), it produces a chain where change begets change. If it does not re-enter, it exists as probability (superposition) until LRU pushes it to COLD and it is extinguished. Either way, there is no need to explicitly manage ownership — the knot's lifespan is its ownership.

    Re-entry = move (Ownership Transfer)

    When a knot re-enters as CAS input, ownership moves from the previous knot to the next. It is not a copy. The previous knot is extinguished and a new knot is created.

    Knot A (cause) --re-entry--> CAS --write--> Knot B (effect)
   |                                            |
   extinction (move complete)                   creation (ownership transferred)

    Because copying is impossible, two effects cannot arise from the same cause. This is the preservation of causality. When a cause is moved to an effect, the cause vanishes and only the effect remains. It cannot be reversed. It is irreversible (Axiom 4). Causality needs no separate declaration — the move of a knot is causality.

The FSM declaration is a completeness statement: the 12 axioms close into a single machine.

    Finite states of the FSM and the infinite degrees of freedom of QFT

    The state set of the FSM (Axiom 13) is {000, 001, 011, 111} — four states, finite. The infinite degrees of freedom in Quantum Field Theory (QFT) refer to field values varying continuously at each point of spacetime. The two do not conflict.

    The four FSM states belong to the OPERATOR side. They describe the states of the operator that tracks which stage CAS is in. The infinite degrees of freedom of QFT belong to the DATA side. They describe the fact that field values recorded in spacetime (classical brackets) are infinite and continuous. In Axiom 1, DATA (classical brackets) and OPERATOR (quantum brackets) are orthogonal, distinct brackets. The FSM describes the finite state transitions of the OPERATOR, while QFT's infinite degrees of freedom describe the space of continuous values recorded in DATA. Because they belong to different layers, there is no conflict.

    What "closed" means

    Closed = nothing to import from outside. The Banya Framework imports nothing beyond its 13 axioms. No 14th axiom is needed. No external constants are needed. No external theories are needed. The axioms alone define the input space, operator, cost, register, output, clock, trigger, multiple projection, and execution model. The FSM completes the transition diagram, and that FSM runs by itself every Planck clock. This is self-completeness. This is closure.

    Guide: Distinguishing Banya Framework from Banya Equation

    What you need to know before reading this Report: the Banya Equation and the Banya Framework are different things.

    What Is the Banya Equation / Banya Framework

    Banya Equation

    $$\delta^{2} = (time + space)^{2} + (observer + superposition)^{2}$$
    delta: change(change) | time: time | space: space | observer: observation | superposition: superposition

    4 words, 2 squares, 1 line. This is the Banya Equation. It is a structural declaration that every change (delta) in the universe is the norm of 4 axes.

    Banya Framework

    It refers to the entire tool system that uses the Banya Equation as its engine, feeds in existing physics equations, substitutes constants, and extracts hidden terms.

    Framework = Equation + transformation rules + sub-frameworks + CAS operator + write theory

    The equation is the engine and the framework is the car. The engine alone can run but cannot drive.

    At-a-Glance Distinction

    Banya EquationBanya Framework
    IdentityOne line of 4-axis orthogonal normEquation + 13 transformation forms + CAS + write theory
    FunctionDeclares structureInserts constants and extracts results
    AnalogyPythagorean theoremAn engineering system that builds structures using the Pythagorean theorem
    StandalonePossible (structure verification)Impossible without the equation
    Exampledelta^2 = c^2 + h-bar^2Insert c, h-bar, G to derive E=mc^2, uncertainty principle, black hole entropy

    A. Common Misconceptions

    Misconception 1. The Banya Equation Is a Theory of Everything (TOE)

    Wrong. The Banya Equation is not a theory but a framework.

    A theory describes "why" and predicts specific numerical values. A framework defines "what is the boundary" and verifies whether existing theories fit within it.

    Theory: E = mc^2 -- if mass is 1kg then energy is 9x10^16 J (numerical prediction)
Framework: delta^2 = c^2 + h-bar^2 -- E = mc^2 is inside the classical bracket (location verification)

    Example: The Pythagorean theorem declares a structure: "the square of the hypotenuse = the sum of the squares of the other two sides." It does not specify whether the sides are 3 or 5. The Banya Equation is the same.

    Misconception 2. The Banya Equation Replaces Existing Physics

    Wrong. Existing physics equations work as-is within the Banya Framework.

    Einstein's E^2 = (mc^2)^2 + (pc)^2 is an app inside the classical bracket. The Schrodinger equation is an app inside the quantum bracket. It is not replacing the apps but discovering the OS on which the apps run.

    Before: relativity app separate, quantum app separate, incompatible
Banya Framework: both apps run on the same OS. Orthogonal, so no conflict

    Example: Excel does not disappear just because Windows was released. Excel runs on Windows.

    Misconception 3. 4 Axes = 4D Spacetime

    Wrong. Spacetime is the 2 axes of the classical bracket: time + space. The other 2 axes (observer, superposition) are the quantum domain. Not all 4 axes are spacetime.

    Classical bracket: time, space -- spacetime (Einstein domain)
Quantum bracket: observer, superposition -- quantum Status (Heisenberg domain)
Orthogonal -- no need to unify

    Example: A car's speedometer and fuel gauge are independent instruments. The fuel gauge does not change automatically when the speedometer goes up. Yet both indicate the car's Status.

    Misconception 4. delta Is Energy

    Wrong. delta is change. Energy is merely one expression of delta.

    delta = change (invariant)
energy = one way to measure change
distance = another way to measure change
probability = another way to measure change

    Example: Whether you measure "distance" in km or miles, the distance itself is the same. Whether you measure delta in energy or probability, the change itself is the same.

    Misconception 5. The + Sign in the Equation Means Addition

    Wrong. The + inside the brackets is a structural notation meaning "two orthogonal axes belong to one bracket." It does not mean to add numbers.

    $$(time + space)^{2} = time^{2} + space^{2}$$
    No cross terms because they are orthogonal

    Example: On a map, going 3km east and 4km north gives a straight-line distance of 5km. Not 3+4=7, but sqrt(9+16)=5. Orthogonal components combine via Pythagoras.

    Misconception 6. Putting Observer as an Axis Is Unscientific

    Quantum mechanics itself has been unable to solve the measurement problem for 100 years. The Copenhagen interpretation, many-worlds interpretation, and decoherence theory have all failed to answer "why does observation change the outcome?"

    The Banya Framework promoted observation from "something to be described" to "an axis of structure." It accepted it without describing it. The same strategy as Einstein, who accepted gravity as spacetime curvature without describing it.

    Einstein: Don't know what gravity is -- define it as spacetime curvature (success)
Banya Framework: Don't know what observation is -- define it as an independent axis (118 PASS)

    Misconception 7. The Units Are Wrong (Neither SI Nor Natural Units)

    The units of the Banya Equation are determined by the left-hand side delta. Neither SI nor natural units. They are delta's units.

    Banya Equation: delta^2 = (time + space)^2 + (observer + superposition)^2

In this equation, time, space, observer, superposition are "Names."
Not m (meters), not s (seconds), not J (joules).
Units are determined only when constants are substituted into the norm.

    Before substituting constants, there are no units. Units appear only after substitution.

    Before SubstitutionAfter SubstitutionUnits
    $\|C\|$$\|C\| = c$m/s
    $\|Q\|$$\|Q\| = \hbar$J·s
    $\delta$$\delta = \sqrt{c^2 + \hbar^2}$Composite units of $c$ and $\hbar$

    Example: Does the word "distance" itself have units? No. You can measure it in km, miles, or light-years. The axes of the Banya Equation are the same. They are just Names, and units attach the moment constants are inserted.

    Wrong: "time is in seconds (s) and space is in meters (m), how can you add them?"
Correct: time and space have no units yet. When c is inserted into the norm, both share the units of c

    In natural units (c=1, h-bar=1), delta = sqrt(2); in SI, delta = sqrt(c^2 + h-bar^2). The framework does not break regardless of unit system. Units are the user's choice, not a property of the framework.

    Misconception 8. The Signs Are Wrong (Minkowski Uses Minus, Why Plus?)

    The Minkowski metric uses minus signs: ds^2 = (ct)^2 - x^2 - y^2 - z^2. But the Banya Equation uses all plus signs. Is that wrong?

    It is not wrong. The Banya Equation is not a physics equation but a structural equation. Signs are determined inside the norm upon substitution.

    Banya Eq:    delta^2 = (time + space)^2 + (observer + superposition)^2
                  Structural declaration. + means "belongs to the same bracket"

Norm substitution: \|C\|^2 = c^2
           How time and space combine with what signs inside
           is determined by the definition of the norm

    Minkowski's minus sign emerges inside the norm:

    $$Expanding \|C\|^2 = c^2$$
    $$(ct)^{2} - x^{2} - y^{2} - z^{2} = ds^{2}$$
    Signs are the internal structure of the norm, not of the Banya Equation
    Banya + : "these axes belong to one bracket" (structure)
Minkowski - : "the norm of time and space combines this way" (internal, after substitution)

They operate at different levels. The Banya Equation declares brackets; signs are determined inside the norm.

    Example: Labeling a drawer "socks" and the method of folding socks are different matters. The Banya Equation is the drawer label; the signs are the folding method. The label does not need to specify the folding method.

    This is precisely why constants must be inserted through the norm. Signs, units, and specific combination methods are all handled inside the norm. The Banya Equation only declares the structure above.

    Misconception 9. It's Circular Reasoning ($E_p = m_p c^2$ is a definition, not a derivation)

    The direction is reversed. It starts from the Write Axiom and arrives at existing physics equations -- not the other way around.

    Wrong direction: We know E = mc² → put it in the framework → "That's what we already knew" (circular)
Actual direction: Write Axiom (cost = ℏ, record = spacetime) → expand → E = mc² emerges (derivation)

    Even if you initialize the Write Axiom as a hypothesis and run it, the same results emerge. If the starting point is different, it's not circular. If a hypothesis produces results consistent with existing physics, the hypothesis is correct.

    Misconception 10. There Are No New Predictions (It merely reinterprets existing values)

    The empty axes among the 4 are the predictions. Each of the 118 physics equations has domains it does not use. Switching to those domains yields previously nonexistent values.

    Coulomb's law: F = kq₁q₂/r² → uses only the space domain
Empty domains: observer, superposition, time
Switching yields: EM decoherence rate, entanglement energy, and other new physical quantities

    See the appendix (118 detailed verifications) "expected derivation values." New physical quantities derivable from empty domains are proposed for each equation. These are predictions unique to the Banya Framework that do not exist in conventional physics.

    Misconception 11. It's Just Relabeling (Just putting new names on existing equations)

    It's not just renaming -- the domain changes. When the domain changes, previously invisible values emerge.

    V = IR (Ohm's law, space domain)
Switch to quantum domain → h/e² = 25,812.807 Ω (quantum Hall resistance)
This value cannot emerge from relabeling alone

    Insert an existing equation into the Banya Framework and switch to an empty domain. Different physical quantities emerge from the same equation. This is the power of a framework.

    B. Usage Cautions

    Caution 1. Do Not Expect Specific Numerical Predictions from the Banya Equation

    The Banya Equation itself only declares structure. To obtain numerical values, go to the Banya Framework and substitute constants.

    Wrong expectation: electron mass should come directly from delta^2 = (time + space)^2 + ...
Correct usage: insert c, h-bar, G -- solve simultaneous equations within the framework -- related values emerge

    The Banya Equation is a map. To ask "how many km from A to B?" by looking at the map, you must first insert the scale (constants).

    Caution 2. Always Compare Framework Results Against Known Physical Values

    Values derived from the framework must be compared against experimentally confirmed physical quantities. If they match, the framework is correct; if not, the substitution process must be reviewed.

    Derived: M_W = 77.5 GeV
Experiment: M_W = 80.4 GeV
Error: 3.5% -- within acceptable range (tree-level approximation)

    The framework is not omnipotent where everything matches. If it is wrong, it is wrong.

    Caution 3. Orthogonal Does Not Mean Combined

    Classical and quantum being orthogonal means "the two are independent." It does not mean to combine them into a single equation.

    Wrong approach: time^2 + observer^2 = ? (mixing axes from different brackets)
Correct approach: time^2 + space^2 = c^2 (trade-off only within the same bracket)

    Just as you cannot add east and height, classical axes and quantum axes must not be directly computed in a single equation. Each bracket is an independent unit.

    Caution 4. What Is Solved and What Remains

    Through Banya Framework recursive substitution, the origin of $\alpha$ = 1/137 and the structure of $\sin^2\theta_W$ have been Solved. Mass ratios for all 3 lepton generations + 6 quarks have been derived.

    ItemIdentityOriginStatus
    α = 1/137.036CAS Compare costDerived from the volume ratio of phase space with 4 domains (axes where Status is recorded) + 3 internal degrees of freedom (cost channels of 1 CAS operation: Read, Compare, Swap) = 7 degrees of freedom. 1/α = 137.036082 (Error 0.00006%)Solved
    $\sin^2\theta_W$ = 0.23122Compare/Read cost ratioSolved. Fundamental formula: $(4\pi^2-3)/(16\pi^2)$ = 0.23101 (0.09%), Running: $3/(4\pi)(1-(4+1/\pi)\alpha)$ = 0.23121 (0.005%)Solved

    Caution 5. Do Not Confuse Equation with Framework

    In conversation, do not say "the Banya Equation predicts." The equation does not predict. The framework derives.

    Wrong: "Predicted Dark energy Ratio using the Banya Equation"
Correct: "Derived Dark energy Ratio by substituting the cosmological constant into the Banya Framework"

    Reason for distinction: saying the equation predicts causes confusion with a theory. The framework is not a theory.

    C. Usage Samples

    All samples follow the same 5 steps.

    #StepAction
    1Banya EquationStart from the original equation delta^2 = (time + space)^2 + (observer + superposition)^2
    2Norm SubstitutionBundle brackets into norms: $\delta^2 = \|C\|^2 + \|Q\|^2$
    3Constant/Hypothesis SubstitutionInitialize by inserting physical constants or hypotheses into the norm
    4Domain TransformationTransform the initialized equation into a specific physics domain

    Example: Think of making pizza -- 1.Knead dough (original equation) 2.Roll into circle (norm substitution) 3.Add toppings (constant substitution) 4.Put in oven (domain transformation) 5.Taste (Verdict). If the order changes, you do not get pizza.

    Sample 1. Deriving Time Dilation (Special Relativity)

    Step 1. Banya Equation

    $$\delta^{2} = (time + space)^{2} + (observer + superposition)^{2}$$

    Step 2. Norm Substitution

    Since the 4 axes are orthogonal, bundle brackets into norms.

    $$\delta^{2} = \|C\|^{2} + \|Q\|^{2}$$
    $\|C\|$ = classical bracket norm, $\|Q\|$ = quantum bracket norm

    Step 3. Constant Substitution

    Insert the speed of light c into the classical bracket norm. The quantum bracket is not used this time, so leave it as is.

    $$\|C\|^{2} = c^{2}$$
    $$\text{i.e., }time^{2} + space^{2} = c^{2}$$
    Speed of light c = 299,792,458 m/s

    Step 4. Domain Transformation -- Object Moving at Velocity v

    Setting space = v (velocity), time is determined.

    time² + v² = c²
time² = c² - v²
time  = √(c² - v²)

    Computing the ratio of time:

    $$time / c = \sqrt{1 - v^{2}/c^{2}}$$

    Step 5. Discovery + Verdict

    This is the time dilation formula of special relativity itself.

    $$\gamma = 1 / \sqrt{1 - v^{2}/c^{2}}$$
    Einstein's Lorentz factor
    At rest (v=0): time = c   -- maximum time
At light speed (v=c): time = 0   -- time stops
The faster you go, the slower time becomes

    Verdict: PASS -- Inserting only a single constant c yielded special relativity.

    Sample 2. Deriving the Uncertainty Principle

    Step 1. Banya Equation

    $$\delta^{2} = (time + space)^{2} + (observer + superposition)^{2}$$

    Step 2. Norm Substitution

    $$\delta^{2} = \|C\|^{2} + \|Q\|^{2}$$

    This time, only the quantum bracket is used.

    $$\|Q\|^{2} = observer^{2} + superposition^{2}$$

    Step 3. Constant Substitution

    Insert the reduced Planck constant h-bar into the quantum bracket norm.

    $$\|Q\|^{2} = \hbar^{2}$$
    $$\text{i.e., }observer^{2} + superposition^{2} = \hbar^{2}$$
    $\hbar$ = 1.055 × 10⁻³⁴ J·s

    Step 4. Domain Transformation -- Trade-off Between Measurement Precision and Superposition Range

    observer and superposition trade off on a circle of radius h-bar.

    Increase observer -- superposition decreases
Make observation more precise -- range of possible superposition narrows

    Converting observer to position measurement precision (related to Delta-x) and superposition to momentum uncertainty (related to Delta-p):

    $$\Delta x \times \Delta p \geq \hbar/2$$

    Step 5. Discovery + Verdict

    This is the Heisenberg uncertainty principle itself.

    Full observation (observer = h-bar): superposition = 0 -- superposition vanishes
No observation (observer = 0): superposition = h-bar -- full superposition

    Verdict: PASS -- Inserting only a single constant h-bar yielded the uncertainty principle.

    TOCTOU Interpretation -- Why the Trade-off

    Above we said "observer and superposition trade off." Why? Because h-bar is the radius of the circle? Correct, but there is a deeper reason.

    CAS is the operator of the quantum bracket (OPERATOR). A lock must be placed to prevent Status from changing between Compare and Swap. The minimum cost of this lock is h-bar. It has the same structure as a TOCTOU lock in computer science.

    Compare position (check Delta-x)
------ momentum may change in between ------
Swap momentum (determine Delta-p)

Lock cost = h-bar/2

    If you Compare position precisely (small Delta-x), more lock cost must be spent on position, leaving less for momentum (Delta-p grows). Total cost must be at least h-bar/2. Nothing can be determined at zero cost. This is the true nature of the uncertainty principle.

    h-bar is not "a mysterious limit of nature." It is the lock cost that protects Status between Compare and Swap. Computation has a cost. That is obvious.

    Sample 3. Deriving E = mc^2 (Write Axiom)

    Step 1. Banya Equation

    $$\delta^{2} = (time + space)^{2} + (observer + superposition)^{2}$$

    Step 2. Norm Substitution

    $$\delta^{2} = \|C\|^{2} + \|Q\|^{2}$$

    Step 3. Constant + Hypothesis Substitution

    This time, 3 constants (c, h-bar, G) and 1 hypothesis (Write Axiom) are inserted.

    Constants: \|C\| = c, \|Q\| = h-bar, gravitational constant G
Hypothesis: "1 write operation consumes all 4 axes by the minimum unit"

    Compute the minimum cost of 1 write using c, h-bar, G:

    $$\text{time cost} = 1 t_p = \sqrt{\hbar G/c^{5}} = 5.391 \times 10^{-44} s$$
    $$\text{energy cost} = 1 E_p = \sqrt{\hbar c^{5}/G} = 1.956 \times 10^{9} J$$
    $$\text{space cost} = 1\, l_p^{2} = \hbar G/c^{3}$$

    Step 4. Domain Transformation -- Converting Write Energy to Mass

    Relationship between the energy (E_p) and time (t_p) of 1 write:

    E_p × t_p = ℏ           ← energy x time of 1 write = h-bar
E_p = ℏ / t_p           ← energy is proportional to the inverse of time
t_p = √(ℏG/c⁵)         ← time cost is determined by c, h-bar, G

Converting to mass:
E_p = m_p × c²          ← m_p = √(ℏc/G) = Planck mass

    For n writes:

    $$E = n \times m_p \times c^{2} = m \times c^{2}$$
    mass $m = n \times m_p$ (number of writes x Planck mass)

    Step 5. Discovery + Verdict

    $$E = mc^{2}$$

    Einstein's mass-energy equivalence formula has emerged. Einstein derived this from the invariance of the speed of light. In the Banya Framework, it is derived from the Write Axiom. The paths are different but the destination is the same.

    Verdict: PASS -- Inserting 3 constants + 1 hypothesis yielded E = mc^2.

    Part 1. Definition and Structure of Banya Framework

    Core Claims of This Report

    $$\delta^{2} = (time + space)^{2} + (observer + superposition)^{2}$$
    delta: change | time: time | space: space | observer: observation | superposition: superposition

    The Banya Framework starts from this single equation and claims and verifies the following:

    Structure: The universe is a structure where 4 domains (time, space, observer, superposition) are orthogonal. The classical bracket (time+space) is DATA (storage, Foreground), and the quantum bracket (observer+superposition) is OPERATOR (operator, Background). The sum of all physical quantities is the amount of change (delta).

    Operator: The sole operator of the universe is CAS (Read, Compare, Swap). 1 CAS operation = quantum of action (h-bar). Equivalence is confirmed across 9 domain transformations. CAS has internal structure in its 3 stages, which structurally matches quark 3 colors, 6 flavors, and 8 gluons.

    Write: Write is a real physical phenomenon. CAS ties a knot on all 4 axes (Swap=space, Read=observer, Compare=superposition, When=time). Eviction (LRU) unties the knot. Gravity = write, entropy = eviction. Causality arises from the logical dependency R, C, S of CAS, and an arrow of time emerges when CAS writes to the time axis. Irreversibility is a property of CAS (OPERATOR), not of time (DATA).

    Domain transformation: The Banya Framework enforces all 4 domains and monitors them all. When existing physics equations use only some domains, switching to the remaining domains reveals hidden physical quantities. Observation is subordinate to change, and all observations are fundamentally indirect. Decoherence is a CAS commit (Background to Foreground transition).

    Unification: The 3-stage costs of CAS correspond to the 4 forces (Swap=gravity, Compare=electromagnetism, Read=weak force, confinement=strong force). A single LRU queue unifies visible matter (HOT 5%), dark matter (WARM 27%), and dark energy (COLD 68%). Inserting constants yields hidden values like a system of simultaneous equations. Input 13, output 24+. More comes out than goes in.

    Verification: Full verification of 118 physics equations, FAIL 0. 6 fundamental physics equations derived from Write Axiom (all 1.000000). Electron charge, Weinberg angle, W/Z mass ratio, Higgs VEV (0.6% Error) derived from CAS cost. Koide Formula 0.0011% Error.

    Chapter 1. Starting Point

    There is a passage in the Heart Sutra:

    "Everything changes except change itself."

    The inventor translated this sentence into mathematics. Change (delta) is invariant. The only thing in the universe that does not change is the "fact of change" itself. This became the left-hand side.

    The right-hand side consists of 4 independent axes that produce change: time and space from classical physics, observer and superposition from quantum physics. These 4 axes are orthogonal. They each contribute to change independently without needing to be combined.

    $$\delta^{2} = (time + space)^{2} + (observer + superposition)^{2}$$
    delta: change | time: time | space: space | observer: observation | superposition: superposition

    4 words, 1 line, 2 squares. This is the Banya Framework. The Banya Framework enforces all 4 domains (time, space, observer, superposition) and monitors them all. When existing physics equations use only some domains, it forcibly opens the remaining domains to reveal hidden physical quantities.

    Core Proposition

    The sum of all physical quantities is the amount of change. Energy, distance, probability, force, intensity -- everything physics measures is another name for change. Each of the 4 axes expresses a different physical quantity, and when combined, they express yet another physical quantity. All together, they sum to delta (change).

    Relation to It-from-Bit

    In physics, there is the information universe theory (It from Bit) that says "the universe is made of information." John Wheeler proposed it and many physicists developed it further. However, the existing information universe theory has a critical problem. It does not define what "information" is, nor how the input/output (I/O) of information works. Saying "the universe is information" without defining what information is amounts to wordplay.

    The Banya Framework solves this problem. Information is a change in state, and state is something accessed via I/O (read/write). The sole operator of the Banya Framework, CAS (Compare-And-Swap: a 3-stage atomic operation of Read, Compare, Swap), defines precisely this I/O. Read is input (I) and Swap is output (O). Compare is the processing stage that checks the input against the expected value. The minimum unit of information is 1 write (= quantum of action h-bar), and the physical cost of this write is quantified (1 t_p, 1 E_p, 1 l_p^2, 1 m_p).

    Existing It-from-Bit: "The universe is information" (no definition of information, no definition of I/O)
    $$\text{Banya Framework:} "The universe is write" (information = state change, I/O = CAS, cost fully quantified)$$
    CAS: Compare-And-Swap

    CAS = Quantum of Action (h-bar) Equivalence Proof

    The sole operator of the Banya Framework, CAS (Read, Compare, Swap), is equivalent to the quantum of action (h-bar) in physics. This is not a metaphor but a mathematical equivalence, confirmed by multiple pieces of evidence through domain transformation.

    Evidence 1: Action of 1 CAS operation = h-bar (direct calculation)

    $$Energy of 1 CAS operation = E_p = 1.9561 \times 10^9 J$$
    $$Time of 1 CAS operation = t_p = 5.3912 \times 10^{-44} s$$
    $$Action of 1 CAS operation = E_p \times t_p = 1.0546 \times 10^-34 J s = \hbar$$
    $$\text{Ratio:} E_p \times t_p / \hbar = 1.000000 (\text{Exact match})$$
    E_p: Planck energy (energy of 1 write) | t_p: Planck time (time of 1 write) | $\hbar$: quantum of action

    The energy x time of 1 CAS operation is exactly h-bar. This is direct evidence that 1 CAS operation is identical to 1 quantum of action.

    Evidence 2: Domain transformation -- from time domain to energy domain

    $$\text{time domain:} 1 CAS operation = 1 t_p (\text{time cost})$$
    $$\text{energy domain:} 1 CAS operation = E_p = \hbar/t_p (\text{energy cost})$$
    $$\text{combined:} E = \hbar \cdot omega -> \text{when CAS frequency} omega = 1/t_p, E = \hbar/t_p = E_p$$
    omega: angular frequency(1/time) | E: energy | Planck-Einstein relation derived from CAS

    Converting CAS ticks in the time domain to the energy domain automatically yields E=h-bar \cdot omega. The time cost of CAS connects to the energy cost via h-bar.

    Evidence 3: Domain transformation -- from space domain to momentum domain

    $$\text{space domain:} 1 CAS operation = 1 l_p (\text{spatial cost})$$
    $$\text{momentum domain:} 1 CAS operation = m_p \times c (\text{momentum cost})$$
    $$\text{combined:} l_p \times m_p \times c = \hbar \rightarrow \Delta x*\Delta p \geq \hbar$$
    $l_p$: Planck length (space of 1 write) | $m_p$: Planck mass | $c$: speed of light | uncertainty principle derived from CAS

    Converting the spatial cost of CAS in the space domain to the momentum domain yields delta-x \cdot delta-p >= h-bar. Since phase space occupancy smaller than 1 CAS operation is impossible, the uncertainty principle is an inevitable consequence of CAS discreteness.

    Evidence 4: Domain transformation -- from mass domain to gravity domain

    $$\text{mass domain:} M = N \times m_p (\text{mass = accumulation of N writes})$$
    $$\text{energy domain:} E = N \times E_p = N \times m_p \times c^2 = Mc^2$$
    $$\text{gravity domain:} r_s = N \times 2l_p = (M/m_p) x 2l_p = 2GM/c^{2}$$
    $M$: mass | $N$: number of writes | $r_s$: Schwarzschild radius | $E=mc^2$ and $r_s=2GM/c^2$ derived simultaneously from CAS

    Switching from the mass domain to the gravity domain yields $E=mc^2$ and $r_s=2GM/c^2$ simultaneously. Mass is the accumulation of CAS operations, and gravity is the spatial budget of accumulated CAS.

    Evidence 5: Domain transformation -- from area domain to information domain

    $$\text{area domain:} 1 CAS operation = 1 l_p^{2} (\text{area cost})$$
    $$\text{information domain:} max CAS count = A / (4 \times l_p^{2}) = \text{number of bits}$$
    $$\text{combined:} S = k_B \times A / (4l_p^{2}) = \text{Bekenstein-Hawking entropy}$$
    $A$: event horizon area | $l_p^2$: Planck area (area of 1 CAS operation) | $S$: entropy | holographic principle derived from CAS

    Switching from the area domain to the information domain yields the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy. The reason entropy is proportional to surface area rather than volume is that CAS occupies 2-dimensional area, not 3-dimensional volume.

    Evidence 6: CAS internal structure -> expansion to quark domain

    CAS internal structure: Read -> Compare -> Swap (3 stages)
    $$\text{quark domain:} 3 colors (R,G,B) = 3 \text{stages} | 6 flavors (3 generations \times 2) = 3 \text{stages} \times success/failure$$
    $$\text{confinement domain:} 8 gluons = 3^{2}-1 | quark confinement = CAS atomicity$$
    Internal structure of CAS 3 stages structurally matches quark physics (hypothesis stage)

    The quantum of action (h-bar) was "the smallest indivisible event" in physics, but had no internal structure. CAS gives this quantum of action the 3-stage internal structure of Read, Compare, Swap. This structure structurally matches the 3 colors, 6 flavors, and 8 gluons of quarks.

    Evidence 7: CAS cost ratio -> expansion to 4-force domain

    $$\text{Swap cost} = \alpha_{G} = 1 (\text{gravity, in Planck units})$$
    $$\text{Compare cost} = \alpha_{em} = 1/137 (\text{electromagnetism})$$

    How to Use Banya Framework

    The Banya Framework is a utility that takes known constants as input and finds hidden terms.

    The core principle is domain transformation. Just as the Fourier transform converts the time domain to the frequency domain to reveal previously invisible patterns, the Banya Framework traverses between the classical domain (time, space) and the quantum domain (observer, superposition) to calculate values not present in existing equations. When a physics equation operates only in a specific domain (sub-frame), switching to the remaining domains reveals the physical quantities hidden there. Since the 4 axes are orthogonal, empty axes always exist, and substituting constants into empty axes yields new values.

    Usage:
  1. Insert known physical constants (initialization)
  2. Check that the framework does not break (framework integrity check)
  3. Switch domains (classical <-> quantum, time <-> space <-> observer <-> superposition)
     Looking at the axis not used by the existing equation reveals hidden terms
  4. Hidden values emerge (new physical quantities from domain transformation)
     Empty domains are also monitored, so values not in the original equation appear
  5. If the result matches existing physics, the framework is correct (quality verification)

    All 4 axes of the Banya Framework are orthogonal. Any physics equation uses only some of the 4 axes. The unused axes are exactly where the hidden values reside. Switching Newton's gravitation (uses only space) to the quantum domain (observer, superposition) yields the gravitational decoherence rate, and switching the Planck-Einstein relation (uses only quantum) to the classical domain (space) yields the de Broglie wavelength. Switching between domains is the key.

    Effect of Enforcing 4 Domains

    Existing physics uses only the domains each equation requires. Newton uses only space, Heisenberg only observer+superposition, Maxwell only time+space. The remaining domains are treated as if they do not exist. The Banya Framework enforces all 4 domains. It applies all 4 axes to every equation. Even empty axes are monitored.

    The effects of this:

    1. Blind spot elimination. Domains invisible to existing physics equations are forcibly revealed. Newtonian mechanics has no observer axis and thus cannot account for the effect of observation on motion. The Banya Framework enforces the observer axis, so the limit where the act of measurement itself disturbs the state of motion (quantum measurement limit) automatically emerges.

    2. Connecting separated theories. Relativity (time+space) and quantum mechanics (observer+superposition) were separate theories for 100 years. Enforcing all 4 axes places both within the same framework, enabling domain switching from one equation to another. Enforcing the quantum domain on the Schwarzschild metric (time+space) yields Hawking radiation, and enforcing the gravity domain on the Schrodinger equation (quantum) yields gravitational phase shift.

    3. Automatic generation of new physical quantities. Substituting constants into empty axes among the 4 determines previously unknown physical quantities like a system of simultaneous equations. The fact that 13 input constants produced 24+ physical quantities as output in this report is the evidence. As long as empty axes exist, new values keep emerging.

    4. Expected derivation values. Each of the 118 equations in the appendix has "expected derivation values." These are unconfirmed physical quantities that may emerge when switching to domains not used by that equation. Enforcing domains automatically generates predictions.
